   * New upstream version 15.8 (LP: #2051151):
     - pe: Align section size up to page size for mem attrs (LP: #2036604)
     - SBAT level: shim,4
     - SBAT policy:
       - Latest: "shim,4\ngrub,3\ngrub.debian,4\n"
       - Automatic: "shim,2\ngrub,3\ngrub.debian,4\n"
       - Note that this does not yet revoke pre NTFS CVE fix GRUB binaries.
   * SECURITY UPDATE: a bug in an error message [LP: #2051151]
     - mok: fix LogError() invocation
     - CVE-2023-40546

     when booting via HTTP [LP: #2051151]
     - avoid incorrectly trusting HTTP headers
     - CVE-2023-40547

     - CVE-2023-40548

shim-dbg_15.8-0ubuntu1_arm64.deb
--------------------------------

 new Debian package, version 2.0.
 size 1376896 bytes: control archive=948 bytes.
     770 bytes,    18 lines      control
     477 bytes,     6 lines      md5sums
 Package: shim-dbg
 Source: shim
 Version: 15.8-0ubuntu1
 Architecture: arm64
 Maintainer: Ubuntu Developers <ubuntu-devel-discuss@lists.ubuntu.com>
 Installed-Size: 6678
 Depends: shim (= 15.8-0ubuntu1)
 Section: debug
 Priority: optional
 Description: boot loader to chain-load signed boot loaders under Secure Boot (dbg symbols)
  This package provides a minimalist boot loader which allows verifying
  signatures of other UEFI binaries against either the Secure Boot DB/DBX or
  against a built-in signature database.  Its purpose is to allow a small,
  infrequently-changing binary to be signed by the UEFI CA, while allowing
  an OS distributor to revision their main bootloader independently of the CA.
  .
  Debug symbols.
 Original-Maintainer: Steve Langasek <vorlon@debian.org>
